  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_30da95ae-a47e-4f78-84e7-5d75229e7856'
      });

  <span id="freeText12638721360035605971" style="display:none">Boy meets boy. Boys become friends. Boys fall in love. An LGBTQ+ graphic novel about life, love, and everything that happens in between: this is the second volume of HEARTSTOPPER, for fans of The Art of Being Normal, Holly Bourne and Love, Simon. <br /><br />Nick and Charlie are best friends. Nick knows Charlie's gay, and Charlie is sure that Nick isn't. <br /><br />But love works in surprising ways, and Nick is discovering all kinds of things about his friends, his family ... and himself. <br /><br />Heartstopper is about friendship, loyalty and mental illness. It encompasses all the small stories of Nick and Charlie's lives that together make up something larger, which speaks to all of us. <br /><br />This is the second volume of Heartstopper, with more to come. Volume two collects all of chapter three from the ongoing web series.</span>

<div id="review_3112430239" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3112430239" />
    <a title="Larry H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5872506-larry-h"><img alt="Larry H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577826084p2/5872506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3112430239?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Larry H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Larry H" href="/user/show/5872506-larry-h">Larry H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3112430239" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4811612655414141877">Good lord, these books are so sweet and so wonderful, I swear my heart grew a few sizes reading this today!<br/><br/>The second volume of Alice Oseman's gorgeous, life-affirming, squee-inducing graphic novel, <b>
  <i>Heartstopper</i>
</b> picks up where the last one left off. Charlie and Nick's friendship has been growing closer and closer, and Charlie definitely has a huge crush on Nick, despite the fact that Nick is straight. Or is he?<br/><br/>Nick can't get Charlie out of his mind. He just wants to be with him, and he's hap</span>
  <span id="freeText4811612655414141877" style="display:none">Good lord, these books are so sweet and so wonderful, I swear my heart grew a few sizes reading this today!<br /><br />The second volume of Alice Oseman's gorgeous, life-affirming, squee-inducing graphic novel, <b>
  <i>Heartstopper</i>
</b> picks up where the last one left off. Charlie and Nick's friendship has been growing closer and closer, and Charlie definitely has a huge crush on Nick, despite the fact that Nick is straight. Or is he?<br /><br />Nick can't get Charlie out of his mind. He just wants to be with him, and he's happiest when they're together. Why can't he stop thinking about him?<br /><br />Charlie's friends are afraid that he's making a mistake falling for a straight guy. Even if Nick is nice to him now, his friends are homophobic bullies, and at some point they figure Nick will turn on Charlie. They don't want to see that happen. Charlie thinks Nick is different. At least he hopes he is.<br /><br />Nick needs to figure out what he wants, and what that means about his identity and his sexuality. Is he gay? Bisexual? Straight? Does he need to make a decision? The one thing he knows is that he wants Charlie.<br /><br />I remember having crushes like this, but when I grew up (in the dark ages) there weren't options to date or even admit you had feelings for someone of the same sex. But I can only imagine that jumble of emotions Charlie and Nick feel. I also remember the internal pressure of trying to define your sexuality, while at the same time trying to convince yourself that your sexuality is only one component of who you are, and it doesn't change everything.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Heartstopper Volume 2</i>
</b> is just so beautiful, warm, and full of emotions. I can't recommend these graphic novels enough, and you can bet I'll pre-order Volume 3 as soon as I can! (It's due out in early February.) Thanks, Alice Oseman, for creating an amazing and utterly necessary story that I can't stop thinking about!! <br /><br />See all of my reviews at <a href="http://itseithersadnessoreuphoria.blogspot.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">itseithersadnessoreuphoria.blogspot.com</a>.<br /><br />You can follow me on Instagram at <a href="https://www.instagram.com/the.bookishworld.of.yrralh/" target="”_blank”" rel="nofollow noopener"> https://www.instagram.com/the.bookishworld.of.yrralh/.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4811612655414141877" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2933019607" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11241707685073739264"><i>"Oh. You're being gay. Good job. Carry on."</i><br/><br/>So, the second installment of this wonderful series was <b>just as wholesome, adorable, inclusive and explorative as the first.</b><br/><br/>In this second volume of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/40495957.Heartstopper_Volume_One__Heartstopper___1_' title='Heartstopper Volume One (Heartstopper, #1) by Alice Oseman' rel='nofollow noopener'>Heartstopper</a>, Nick and Charlie are officially in love and cute as fuck, but of course not everything is easy just because of that. No, Nick is still figuring himself out, and the two of them have to come to terms with how, when and to who they want to come out to - if at all.<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7789423.Alice_Oseman' title='Alice Oseman' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alice Oseman</a> keeps doing an amaz</span>
  <span id="freeText11241707685073739264" style="display:none"><i>"Oh. You're being gay. Good job. Carry on."</i><br /><br />So, the second installment of this wonderful series was <b>just as wholesome, adorable, inclusive and explorative as the first.</b><br /><br />In this second volume of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/40495957.Heartstopper_Volume_One__Heartstopper___1_" title="Heartstopper Volume One (Heartstopper, #1) by Alice Oseman" rel="nofollow noopener">Heartstopper</a>, Nick and Charlie are officially in love and cute as fuck, but of course not everything is easy just because of that. No, Nick is still figuring himself out, and the two of them have to come to terms with how, when and to who they want to come out to - if at all.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7789423.Alice_Oseman" title="Alice Oseman" rel="nofollow noopener">Alice Oseman</a> keeps doing an amazing job with the dialogue, that goes amazing with her simple art, while also delivering on all other fonts such as tension, fluffiness and inclusivity - as a bisexual baby myself, I love and relate to Nick a lot.<br /><br />Something I really appreciate too is that these characters here actually <i>communicate with each other.</i> There are some misunderstandings sometimes because we humans are weird and complicated, but they quickly get resolved because Charlie, Nick and their friends actually talk to each other. It's something so small but so nice to read about.<br /><br />Again, this is lovely. I actually can't believe that it isn't even more talked about - <b>this is the kind of content we queers want and need.</b></span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Z9jA6SAQRvAyOZ8VuQngWIzO/k0jBO3cYwMPOV8WOAV5At3HKOwLb0wqEH2LMIC75MoxxWswQdK3bxftkYBerQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('i9u6WURTOMTCh6Xlm3/L44TwSBcUBm+TS1+DcnvtbKuVAad3TK91W7yUKo2pRqsA7PSHn1wyw52fM5umtXsKAw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1899486248111403612">Alice Oseman is an author/illustrator and was born in 1994 in Kent, England. She has written four YA contemporary novels about teenage disasters: SOLITAIRE, RADIO SILENCE, I WAS BORN FOR THIS, and LOVELESS. She is also the creator of LGBTQ+ YA romance webcomic HEARTSTOPPER, which is now published in physical form by Hachette Children's Books.<br/><br/>Alice’s first novel SOLITAIRE was published when she was</span>
  <span id="freeText1899486248111403612" style="display:none">Alice Oseman is an author/illustrator and was born in 1994 in Kent, England. She has written four YA contemporary novels about teenage disasters: SOLITAIRE, RADIO SILENCE, I WAS BORN FOR THIS, and LOVELESS. She is also the creator of LGBTQ+ YA romance webcomic HEARTSTOPPER, which is now published in physical form by Hachette Children's Books.<br /><br />Alice’s first novel SOLITAIRE was published when she was nineteen. Her YA novels have been nominated for the YA Book Prize, the Inky Awards, and the Goodreads Choice Award, and HEARTSTOPPER has been optioned for TV. She can usually be found staring aimlessly at computer screens, questioning the meaninglessness of existence, or doing anything and everything to avoid getting an office job.</span>

      $('bookCover_53344030').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
